<p>如果当前处于用户未授权状态，调用该接口注入事件不生效。</p> <p>从API version 20开始，建议先使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#oh_input_requestinjection">OH_Input_RequestInjection</a>请求授权。然后通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#oh_input_queryauthorizedstatus">OH_Input_QueryAuthorizedStatus</a>查询授权状态，当授权状态为<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_injectionstatus">AUTHORIZED</a>时，再使用该接口。</p> <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.MultimodalInput.Input.Core</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 12</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.35.10.1.3.1.1" width="50%">参数项</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.35.10.1.3.1.2" width="50%">描述</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">const struct <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-input-input-keyevent">Input_KeyEvent</a>* keyEvent</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>按键事件对象，通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#oh_input_createkeyevent">OH_Input_CreateKeyEvent</a>接口可以创建按键事件对象。</p> <p>使用完需使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#oh_input_destroykeyevent">OH_Input_DestroyKeyEvent</a>接口销毁按键事件对象。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> class="linenums"><li>Input_Result <span class="hljs-built_in">OH_Input_RequestInjection</span>(Input_InjectAuthorizeCallback callback)</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>当前应用申请注入权限，包括申请注入按键事件<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#oh_input_injectkeyevent">OH_Input_InjectKeyEvent</a>、注入触屏输入事件<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#oh_input_injectmouseevent">OH_Input_InjectMouseEvent</a>等注入操作的权限。</p> <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.MultimodalInput.Input.Core</p> <p><strong>设备行为差异</strong>：该接口仅在PC/2in1设备上生效，在其他设备上返回801错误码。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 20</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.84.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">参数项</th> <th href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_injectauthorizecallback">Input_InjectAuthorizeCallback</a> callback</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">授权状态回调，具体请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_injectauthorizecallback">Input_InjectAuthorizeCallback</a>。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.84.11.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.84.11.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_result">Input_Result</a></td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>返回结果码，参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_result">Input_Result</a>。</p> <p> INPUT_SUCCESS = 0 申请授权成功，等待用户授权结果并回调授权状态。</p> <p> INPUT_PARAMETER_ERROR = 401 参数错误，参数callback为空。</p> <p> INPUT_DEVICE_NOT_SUPPORTED = 801 表示不支持该功能。</p> <p> INPUT_SERVICE_EXCEPTION = 3800001 服务器错误。</p> <p> INPUT_INJECTION_AUTHORIZING = 3900005 正在授权中。</p> <p> INPUT_INJECTION_OPERATION_FREQUENT = 3900006 重复请求（当前应用连续申请授权弹窗成功，间隔时间不超过3秒）。</p> <p> INPUT_INJECTION_AUTHORIZED = 3900007 当前应用已经授权。</p> <p> INPUT_INJECTION_AUTHORIZED_OTHERS = 3900008 其它应用已经授权。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div>  <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 816px;"><h3 id="oh_input_queryauthorizedstatus" href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-axis-type-h#inputevent_axistype">InputEvent_AxisType</a> axisType</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">轴类型，具体请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-axis-type-h#inputevent_axistype">InputEvent_AxisType</a>。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">double* axisValue</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">出参，返回轴事件的值，正数向前滚动（例如，1.0表示向前滚动一个单位），负数向后滚动（例如，-1.0表示向后滚动一个单位）,零表示没有滚动。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.95.10.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.95.10.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_result">Input_Result</a></td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">若获取轴事件指定轴类型的轴值成功，则返回<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_result">INPUT_SUCCESS</a>；若axisEvent或者axisValue为NULL，则返回<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_result">INPUT_PARAMETER_ERROR</a>。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div>  <div class="tiledSection" width="50%">要监听的轴事件类型，轴事件类型定义在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-axis-type-h#inputevent_axiseventtype">InputEvent_AxisEventType</a>中。</td> </tr> <tr><td href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_result">INPUT_OCCUPIED_BY_SYSTEM</a> 该快捷键已被系统占用，可以通过接口<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#oh_input_getallsystemhotkeys">OH_Input_GetAllSystemHotkeys</a>查询所有的系统快捷键。</p> <p> <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_result">INPUT_OCCUPIED_BY_OTHER</a> 已被抢占订阅。</p> <p> <a class="cellrowborder" width="50%">deviceInfo 指向输入设备信息<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-input-input-deviceinfo">Input_DeviceInfo</a>的指针。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-cpp" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-type">int32_t</span> <span class="hljs-title">OH_Input_InjectTouchEvent</span><span class="hljs-params">(<span class="hljs-type">const</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> Input_TouchEvent* touchEvent)</span></span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>使用以指定屏幕左上角为原点的相对坐标系的坐标注入触屏输入事件。</p> <p>如果当前处于用户未授权状态，调用该接口注入事件不生效。</p> <p>从API version 20开始，建议先使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#oh_input_requestinjection">OH_Input_RequestInjection</a>请求授权。然后通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#oh_input_queryauthorizedstatus">OH_Input_QueryAuthorizedStatus</a>查询授权状态，当授权状态为<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_injectionstatus">AUTHORIZED</a>时，再使用该接口。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 12</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.150.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">参数项</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.150.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">描述</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">const struct <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-input-input-touchevent">Input_TouchEvent</a>* touchEvent</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>触屏输入事件对象，通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#oh_input_createtouchevent">OH_Input_CreateTouchEvent</a>接口可以创建触屏输入事件对象。</p> <p>使用完需使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#oh_input_destroytouchevent">OH_Input_DestroyTouchEvent</a>接口销毁触屏输入事件对象。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.150.11.1.3.1.1" href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#oh_input_requestinjection">OH_Input_RequestInjection</a>请求授权。然后通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#oh_input_queryauthorizedstatus">OH_Input_QueryAuthorizedStatus</a>查询授权状态，当授权状态为<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_injectionstatus">AUTHORIZED</a>时，再使用该接口。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 20</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.159.9.1.3.1.1" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1080px;"><h3 id="oh_input_addkeyeventhook" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">OH_Input_AddKeyEventHook()<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="oh_input_addkeyeventhook" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-scss" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>Input_Result <span class="hljs-built_in">OH_Input_AddKeyEventHook</span>(Input_KeyEventCallback callback)</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>添加一个按键事件拦截钩子函数。</p> <p>添加后可以通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#oh_input_removekeyeventhook">OH_Input_RemoveKeyEventHook</a>接口移除。一个进程仅支持设置一个钩子，一个应用支持多个钩子函数，后添加的生效优先级更高。</p> <p>在使用该接口之前，需要用户在设备的“设置”-&gt;“隐私和安全”-&gt;“权限管理”中打开“键盘输入辅助”权限。该权限仅PC/2in1、Tablet设备支持。</p> <p><strong>需要权限：</strong> ohos.permission.HOOK_KEY_EVENT</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 21</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.170.10.1.3.1.1" width="50%">参数项</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.170.10.1.3.1.2" width="50%">描述</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_keyeventcallback">Input_KeyEventCallback</a> callback</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">钩子函数，用于拦截待分发的所有按键事件。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.170.12.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.170.12.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_result">Input_Result</a></td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>OH_Input_AddKeyEventHook的执行结果：</p> <p> <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_result">INPUT_SUCCESS</a> 表示操作成功。</p> <p> <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_result">INPUT_PARAMETER_ERROR</a> 表示参数检查失败。</p> <p> <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_result">INPUT_DEVICE_NOT_SUPPORTED</a> 表示不支持该功能。 </p> <p> <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_result">INPUT_PERMISSION_DENIED</a> 表示权限验证失败。</p> <p> <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_result">INPUT_REPEAT_INTERCEPTOR</a> 表示重复设置钩子。一个进程仅支持设置一个钩子。</p> <p> <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_result">INPUT_SERVICE_EXCEPTION</a> 表示服务异常，请重试。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div>  <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 864px;"><h3 id="oh_input_removekeyeventhook" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">OH_Input_RemoveKeyEventHook()<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="oh_input_removekeyeventhook" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-scss" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>Input_Result <span class="hljs-built_in">OH_Input_RemoveKeyEventHook</span>(Input_KeyEventCallback callback)</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>移除按键事件拦截钩子函数。</p> <p>通常与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#oh_input_addkeyeventhook">OH_Input_AddKeyEventHook</a>接口配合使用。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 21</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.171.8.1.3.1.1" width="50%">参数项</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.171.8.1.3.1.2" width="50%">描述</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_keyeventcallback">Input_KeyEventCallback</a> callback</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">钩子函数，用于拦截待分发的所有按键事件。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.171.10.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.171.10.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_result">Input_Result</a></td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>OH_Input_RemoveKeyEventHook的执行结果：</p> <p> <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_result">INPUT_SUCCESS</a> 表示操作成功。如果之前没有添加对应钩子，移除时也会返回成功。</p> <p> <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_result">INPUT_PARAMETER_ERROR</a> 表示参数检查失败。</p> <p> <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_result">INPUT_SERVICE_EXCEPTION</a> 表示服务异常，请重试。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div>  <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1104px;"><h3 id="oh_input_dispatchtonexthandler" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">OH_Input_DispatchToNextHandler()<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="oh_input_dispatchtonexthandler" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-iiq-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-scss" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>Input_Result <span class="hljs-built_in">OH_Input_DispatchToNextHandler</span>(int32_t eventId)</li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>重新分发按键事件。</p> <p>只有被钩子拦截的按键事件才能被重新分发，重新分发的事件必须保持原有优先级顺序。</p> <p>调用该接口后，按键事件可在3秒内重新分发。如果超过3秒，将返回<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_result">INPUT_PARAMETER_ERROR</a>。</p> <p>重新分发的事件需要保证配对关系。如果重新分发了一个或多个按键按下事件<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_keyeventaction">KEY_ACTION_DOWN</a>，再重新分发按键抬起事件<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_keyeventaction">KEY_ACTION_UP</a>或按键动作取消事件<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_keyeventaction">KEY_ACTION_CANCEL</a>可以成功。</p> <p>如果仅分发<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_keyeventaction">KEY_ACTION_UP</a>或<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_keyeventaction">KEY_ACTION_CANCEL</a>按键事件，接口可以调用成功，但不会执行实际的分发动作。</p> <p>如果分发的事件未被钩子拦截，函数调用会成功，但不会执行实际的分发动作。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 21</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.172.12.1.3.1.1" width="50%">参数项</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.172.12.1.3.1.2" width="50%">描述</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">int32_t eventId</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">按键事件的ID。可以通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#oh_input_getkeyeventid">OH_Input_GetKeyEventId</a>接口获取。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>返回：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.172.14.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.172.14.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_result">Input_Result</a></td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>OH_Input_DispatchToNextHandler的执行结果：</p> <p> <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_result">INPUT_SUCCESS</a> 表示操作成功。</p> <p> <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_result">INPUT_PARAMETER_ERROR</a> 表示参数检查失败。可通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#oh_input_getkeyeventid">OH_Input_GetKeyEventId</a>查看传入的eventId是否准确。</p> <p> <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-oh-input-manager-h#input_result">INPUT_SERVICE_EXCEPTION</a> 表示服务异常，请重试。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div> </div> <div></div></div>
